[owner isValid]
The block will never be called. This is because we are observing the 'valid' key on self without passing NSKeyValueObservingOptionPrior _AND_ and the same time passing 'self' as the 'owner'. Since 'self' is the 'owner', when -invalidate is called it will cancel the token before -willChangeValueForKey: is called. The solution is to pass the NSKeyValueObservingOptionPrior option when creating the token. owner: %@
